***meert.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meert</a> (64043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marter.html>marter</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">murd</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meert</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meert.html>meerten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Groningen<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">polecat</span>
<ul><li><b>1914</b> February 2, "<a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>Over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> Dialect, XI.", <i>Nieuwsblad <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noorden.html>Noorden</a></i>, second part.

***meester.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meester.html>meester</a> (1104)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mêester</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mēster</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*maester</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:magister.html>magister</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meester.html>meester</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meesters.html>meesters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meestertje.html>meestertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>master</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rail transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> train driver</li></ol>

<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">medezingen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">medesingen</i>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meezingen.html>meezingen</a></strong>
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:meezingen.html>meezingen</a></b>

***meid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a> (700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meit</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meget</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*megith</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*magath</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*magaþs</i>. Compare also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maagd.html>maagd</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meiden.html>meiden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meiske.html>meiske</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meidje.html>meidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>girl, <a href = vnd.unilang:lass.html>lass</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meiden.html>meiden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgelopen.html>afgelopen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaterdag.html>zaterdag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> zwemwedstrijd.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a swimming match last Saturday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>Goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a></b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Well done, <b>girl</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>maid
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bode.html>bode</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deerne.html>deerne</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienstbode.html>dienstbode</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienstmaagd.html>dienstmaagd</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Commonly used as an address for female <a href = vnd.unilang:pets.html>pets</a>, especially female dogs.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brave.html>Brave</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a></b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Good <b>girl</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Use in the singular may connote fortitude, bravery or acting like a grown-up, but it may also connote vulgarity or subservience due to the meaning “maid”. These connotations are much weaker in the plural, which can be used neutrally with little regard for context.</li>
<li>Use for adult women (and to a lesser degree for older adolescent <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often considered patronising, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> especially true of the diminutives.</li>
<li>The diminutive <i><a href = vnd.unilang:meidje.html>meidje</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> uncommon; the regular diminutive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a></i> along with its variants <i><a href = vnd.unilang:meiske.html>meiske</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:meisie.html>meisie</a></i>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienstmeid.html>dienstmeid</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">huismeid</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">keukenmeid</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">meis</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:informeel.html>informeel</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:jonge.html>jonge</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meiden.html>meiden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lol.html>lol</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:verouderd.html>verouderd</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkster.html>werkster</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dienstmeisje.html>dienstmeisje</a></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:meier.html>meier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head of the household personnel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">māior</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">greater</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, short for <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">maior <a href = vnd.unilang:domus.html>domus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">supervisor of a house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">מאה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méye</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">מֵאָה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>'á</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hundred</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:honderdje.html>honderdje</a></i>, a 100 <a href = vnd.unilang:guilder.html>guilder</a> banknote, nowadays, however less frequently, used for a 100 euro banknote</li></ol>

***melaatse.html

<p>Inflected form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melaats.html>melaats</a></i> (see there for more), which derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">malaetsch</i>.

***melaatsheid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:melaatsheid.html>melaatsheid</a> (68778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">malaetscheit</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melaats.html>melaats</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">leprose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ity, -ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> skin disease; either leprosy (the infectious skin-disease caused by the bacteria <i>Mycobacterium leprae</i>) or <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> another disease historically conflated with leprosy</li></ol>

***melasse.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:melasse.html>melasse</a> (56708)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">melaza</i> (possibly <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> cognate <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mélasse</i>), ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:mel.html>mel</a></i> 'honey, sweet stuff', cognate with English, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">melaço</i> etc.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melasse.html>melasse</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melasse.html>melassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melasse.html>melassetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>the thick brownish syrup molasses, the remnant after refining raw sugar (cane)</li></ol>

***melden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:melden.html>melden</a> (2220)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:melden.html>melden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*meldon</i> (attested in <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">maltho</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I declare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*meldōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melden.html>melden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to report, communicate; let know</li></ol>

***melk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:melk.html>melk</a> (1639)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">melc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">miluk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*meluks</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂melǵ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melk.html>melk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>milk <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">nutritious liquid produced by a lactating mammalian mother</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Various resembling 'milky' juices, as secreted by certain plants and insects</li></ol>

***melkmuil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:melkmuil.html>melkmuil</a> (56706)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melk.html>melk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">milk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muil.html>muil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">muzzle, face</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="Latn" lang="en">milksop</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melkmuil.html>melkmuil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melkmuilen.html>melkmuilen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:melkmuil.html>melkmuiltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An immature person, notably an ignorant novice; <span class="Latn" lang="en">greenhorn</span>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meloen.html>meloen</a> (14817)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">melone</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">melon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">melon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mēlō</i>, shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mēlopepō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Koine_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Koine Greek">Koine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μηλοπέπων</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mēlopépōn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:membraan.html>membraan</a> (53886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">membrane</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">membrana</i>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">membra</i>, plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">membrum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">member, limb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-anus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:membraan.html>membraan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:membranen.html>membranen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:membraan.html>membraantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A membrane, thin, often separating, layer of (skin or other) tissue in animal or plant anatomy
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlies.html>vlies</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>An artefact similar in function and/or construction, e.g. as mechanical part</li></ol>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">membraanleder</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">membraanleer</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>

***men.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> (691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></i>, an unstressed variety of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Accordingly, originally pronounced with <span class="IPA">[ə]</span>; now predominantly with a full vowel <span class="IPA">[ɛ]</span>, especially in those areas where the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> chiefly literary. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">indefinite pronoun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">indefinite<span class="ib-comma">,</span> subject</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One, you, they, everyone; humanity, (the) people, the public opinion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zegt.html>zegt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>...</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>People</b> say that.... It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> that...</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeuren.html>gebeuren</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>You</b> never know what’s going to happen.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>When not used as a subject, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></i> must be replaced with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">you</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or sometimes <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">them</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>The word as such <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very common in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Limburg_(Netherlands)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Limburg (Netherlands)">Limburg</a> and some other areas, where it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> part of the local dialects. Elsewhere it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not downright <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> but perceived as formal and predominantly replaced with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> as a subject (similarly to English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">one</i>).</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niemand.html>niemand</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mennen.html>mennen</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mennen.html>mennen</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr />

***meneer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meneer.html>meneer</a> (224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijnheer.html>mijnheer</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mijnhere</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">my</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lord</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, formed similarly to English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:milord.html>milord</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meneer.html>meneer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meneren.html>meneren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meneertje.html>meneertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:meneer.html>meneer</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:formele.html>formele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:manier.html>manier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spreken.html>spreken</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>Dag</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meneer.html>meneer</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vries.html>Vries</a>!</i> </li></ul></dd>
<dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i>`Heeft <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigenaar.html>eigenaar</a>?' <a href = vnd.unilang:vroeg.html>vroeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a>.<br /> `Onlangs <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Grand <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>Hotel</a> Europa <a href = vnd.unilang:overgegaan.html>overgegaan</a> in Chinese <a href = vnd.unilang:handen.html>handen</a>,' <a href = vnd.unilang:zei.html>zei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a>.
